enables consumer groups to persist and retrieve committed offsets for topic partitions. The architecture spans multiple layers from protocol definitions to broker-side coordination.\\n\\n### Core Offset Storage\\n\\nThe `__consumer_offsets` internal topic is the central repository for all consumer group offset information. The OffsetAndMetadata class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java) serves as the server-side representation of committed offsets, storing the offset value, optional leader epoch, and custom metadata. This is complemented by the client-side OffsetAndMetadata class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java) that consumers use to commit offsets.\\n\\n### GroupCoordinator Architecture\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinator interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) defines the contract for offset management operations. It's implemented by GroupCoordinatorService (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java), which delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard instances for distributed coordination. The GroupCoordinatorShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java) manages in-memory state for specific topic partitions.\\n\\n### Offset Management Operations\\n\\n**Offset Commit Handler**: The OffsetMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java) is responsible for handling offset commits. It validates commit requests, updates offset state, and persists offset records to the __consumer_offsets topic. The GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java) provides utilities for creating and converting offset commit records, including legacy format support.\\n\\n**Offset Fetch Handler**: When clients request to fetch committed offsets, the OffsetMetadataManager's fetchOffsets method retrieves the stored offsets from its in-memory state. The fetchOffsets operation in GroupCoordinatorShard coordinates the retrieval and formats responses according to the protocol version.\\n\\n**Offset Deletion**: The deleteOffsets method in OffsetMetadataManager handles offset deletion requests, creating tombstone records for offset keys to remove them during log compaction.\\n\\n### Request/Response Protocol\\n\\nThe OffsetCommitRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitRequest.java) and OffsetCommitResponse (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitResponse.java) classes handle the protocol for committing offsets. Similarly, OffsetFetchRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchRequest.java) and OffsetFetchResponse (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchResponse.java) handle offset retrieval, and OffsetDeleteRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetDeleteRequest.java) supports offset deletion via the admin API.\\n\\n### Broker-Side Request Handling\\n\\nThe KafkaApis.scala file (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaApis.scala) contains the broker-level handlers: handleOffsetCommitRequest, handleOffsetFetchRequest, and handleOffsetDeleteRequest. These handlers parse protocol requests, perform authorization checks, and delegate to the GroupCoordinator for actual offset operations.\\n\\n### Client-Side Offset Management\\n\\nThe ConsumerCoordinator (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerCoordinator.java) manages offset commit operations on the consumer side. The CommitRequestManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CommitRequestManager.java) handles queueing and retrying of offset commit requests. The OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker.java) invokes user callbacks upon successful offset commits.\\n\\n### Group Types and Offset Management\\n\\nBoth ClassicGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) and ConsumerGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java) implement the Group interface and support offset management operations. The GroupMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java) manages group membership state and coordinates with the OffsetMetadataManager for offset operations.\\n\\n### Offset Expiry and Compaction\\n\\nOffsets are automatically expired based on retention policy configured in GroupCoordinatorConfig (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorConfig.java). The LogCleanerManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleanerManager.java) handles log compaction of the __consumer_offsets topic, removing expired offset records via tombstones.\\n\\n### Metrics and Monitoring\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinatorMetrics (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/metrics/GroupCoordinatorMetrics.java) and GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/metrics/GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard.java) track offset commit operations. enables consumer groups to persist and retrieve committed offsets for topic partitions. The architecture spans multiple layers from protocol definitions to broker-side coordination.\\n\\n### Core Offset Storage\\n\\nThe `__consumer_offsets` internal topic is the central repository for all consumer group offset information. The OffsetAndMetadata class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java) serves as the server-side representation of committed offsets, storing the offset value, optional leader epoch, and custom metadata. This is complemented by the client-side OffsetAndMetadata class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java) that consumers use to commit offsets.\\n\\n### GroupCoordinator Architecture\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinator interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) defines the contract for offset management operations. It's implemented by GroupCoordinatorService (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java), which delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard instances for distributed coordination. The GroupCoordinatorShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java) manages in-memory state for specific topic partitions.\\n\\n### Offset Management Operations\\n\\n**Offset Commit Handler**: The OffsetMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java) is responsible for handling offset commits. It validates commit requests, updates offset state, and persists offset records to the __consumer_offsets topic. The GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java) provides utilities for creating and converting offset commit records, including legacy format support.\\n\\n**Offset Fetch Handler**: When clients request to fetch committed offsets, the OffsetMetadataManager's fetchOffsets method retrieves the stored offsets from its in-memory state. The fetchOffsets operation in GroupCoordinatorShard coordinates the retrieval and formats responses according to the protocol version.\\n\\n**Offset Deletion**: The deleteOffsets method in OffsetMetadataManager handles offset deletion requests, creating tombstone records for offset keys to remove them during log compaction.\\n\\n### Request/Response Protocol\\n\\nThe OffsetCommitRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitRequest.java) and OffsetCommitResponse (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitResponse.java) classes handle the protocol for committing offsets. Similarly, OffsetFetchRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchRequest.java) and OffsetFetchResponse (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchResponse.java) handle offset retrieval, and OffsetDeleteRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetDeleteRequest.java) supports offset deletion via the admin API.\\n\\n### Broker-Side Request Handling\\n\\nThe KafkaApis.scala file (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaApis.scala) contains the broker-level handlers: handleOffsetCommitRequest, handleOffsetFetchRequest, and handleOffsetDeleteRequest. These handlers parse protocol requests, perform authorization checks, and delegate to the GroupCoordinator for actual offset operations.\\n\\n### Client-Side Offset Management\\n\\nThe ConsumerCoordinator (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerCoordinator.java) manages offset commit operations on the consumer side. The CommitRequestManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CommitRequestManager.java) handles queueing and retrying of offset commit requests. The OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker.java) invokes user callbacks upon successful offset commits.\\n\\n### Group Types and Offset Management\\n\\nBoth ClassicGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) and ConsumerGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java) implement the Group interface and support offset management operations. The GroupMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java) manages group membership state and coordinates with the OffsetMetadataManager for offset operations.\\n\\n### Offset Expiry and Compaction\\n\\nOffsets are automatically expired based on retention policy configured in GroupCoordinatorConfig (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorConfig.java). The LogCleanerManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleanerManager.java) handles log compaction of the __consumer_offsets topic, removing expired offset records via tombstones.\\n\\n### Metrics and Monitoring\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinatorMetrics (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/metrics/GroupCoordinatorMetrics.java) and GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/metrics/GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard.java) track offset commit operations.
